name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted October 2, 2023
msg:This time I chose this hotel because I was going to watch a concert at the Sports Center:
1. Let's talk about the location first. The location of the hotel is really good. It is very suitable for watching concerts. It is only a few minutes' walk from the Library Station of Metro Line 3 and 4. After the concert, there is a free shuttle bus that takes you directly to the Library Station. You can walk a little distance to the hotel. In addition, it is not far from the new Anhui Museum and Swan Lake;
2. Let's talk about the hardware. It should be an old five-star hotel. The hardware is not bad, but the style is old-fashioned. Some equipment has not kept up with the times. For example, the TV, telephone, and hair dryer are all old-fashioned. The toilet is not smart. There is a small refrigerator, but there is no free mini bar. Except for a small bottle of mineral water, everything else is charged. The pillow is also soft and low. The sound insulation effect is not good. At two or three o'clock in the morning, there were children running around in the corridor and were woken up. But this cannot be blamed on the hotel. It is mainly because the quality of the guests is not good;
3. After talking about the hardware, let's talk about the software. I want to complain about the front desk service. When checking in, the two girls at the front desk seemed to be half asleep, and their attitude was very average. Even the service attitude of ordinary comfortable hotels was better than them. I didn't feel a smile or enthusiasm, which was not in line with the star rating and price of the hotel. It really needs training and upgrading. In addition to the service awareness, the work was not detailed enough. Two of us checked in, and for the convenience of travel, we asked for two room cards, but one of them was not entered into the system before it was given to us, resulting in one room card not being able to be used normally. Another difference between the front desk and the five-star hotel is that usually when there are not many guests staying, the hotel will give a better room or upgrade, but the front desk only gave the lowest floor of the same level room type, and the view was not good, not to mention the upgrade (of course, the upgrade is not the hotel's obligation, and we have no such requirement). Except for the poor service at the front desk, the services of other staff were good, especially the concierge uncle in the lobby, who always greeted guests with a smile and took the initiative to show the way. The service of the girl in the executive lounge was also good, and the cleaning lady also cleaned the room very well;
4. In other aspects, because we did not eat breakfast in the hotel, the room we booked did not include breakfast, so we could not comment on the quality of the breakfast; there is an underground garage, and guests can park for free.
Overall, except for the front desk service which needs to be improved, everything else is good.
